The dryers as well seem to be a new condition. The laundromat looks pretty new but it is cramped due to its location. So expect a lot of cramped room in between the aisles. The machines accept coins bills and also credit or debit cards and there's also a loyalty card available that offers bonus credits. One downside is that they do charge to use the restroom but that's sort of the norm for most laundromats. Parking is somewhat of an inconvenience because there are handicap spots available in the front but not too many general parking spaces in front of the laundromat. There are a few parking spots behind the laundromat but not many. The place does have Wi-Fi and you'll need a password. Nice looking and clean with efficient machines that are
reasonably priced.

However, if you use your credit or debit card the machines will take extra money off of your card without your knowledge.  My wife and I came to wash a single load of laundry using a $2 machine.  Our bank account shows we were charged $2.18 AND AN ADDITIONAL $10.  I immediately called the posted phone no. and it went straight to voicemail.  The posted sign also said the nearby Cricket store would help if needed so I went there to complain.  The man there told me there was an attendant at the laundry mat but when I talked to her she told me that in fact the man at the store was the owner.  When I went back to the Cricket store and confronted him about the $10 charge he started talking about how only temporary but I told him that doesn't matter.  You can't just take $10 out of people's account without their knowledge.  He started some assinine explanation about how restaurants do the same thing (how ironic that we had just come from a restaurant where that DIDN'T HAPPEN), but I cut him off and told him (yelled it really) as I was exiting his store he needs to post signs warning people that his is taking their money "temporarily".

On another review site, a one star reviewer complained that when she bought a $20 fastcard, the machine TOOK AN ADDITIONAL $20 FROM HER ACCOUNT.

This is not an honest and respectable business practice.  People should not only boycott this store but they should actively work to put this charlatan out of business unless he stops taking people's money without their knowledge.<//Review>

I waited some time before posting this review because I didn't want Sammy the manager to try and cancel our refund. ANYWAY it won't take you too long to find bad reviews about this place that tell you how rude, unfriendly and INCONSIDERATE these people are towards there customers. My name is Marco, and my personal experience with them started off...well...bland and awkward but still not "horrible" (that comes later). My wife and I found quite a variety of very cheap sofas and bedspreads, the young man came to greet us, no smile, no hand shaking, no welcoming feeling really he simply approached us and asked "hello? Are you looking for furniture?" I was a little caught of guard by his lack of rapport building but decided to ignore it for the sake of cheap prices. We found a couch we liked on a Monday and decided to buy it full price. They didn't have it so had to be ordered, it took only a couple days to be delivered to their store. On Wednesday, when it arrived, I receive a call from an older man who's message for me was "yeah hi, this Marco? We have your couch. Please pick up as soon as possible" not friendly not asking me to do it, simply rude and sounded like he was annoyed that my couch was there. I show up and there are two unprofessional looking older gentlemen at a table, the drivers. I walk in, no one greets me, no says anything as I just sorta stand by at the greeting desk. Not until I literally cleared my throat and ask if i can pick up a coach I ordered. One of the "gentleman" gets up doesn't say a word, simply gestures to follow him. He takes me to a damaged box and says "this is the one" and walks away. The box has scratches and Knicks but WORST OF ALL the actual couch was damaged. A big ole hole right at the base of the front of the couch was there. I was shocked that he even tried to give this to me! I re-enter their shop and I let them know (as if he didn't know) that the couch is damaged. The guy, frustrated, gets up and goes to investigate. His response? He turns to one of his drivers and says "go get me staple gun"...wow...really? He then continues to STAB SILVER STAPLES into my BLACK COUCH. right in the front there, then he has the nerve to ask "you have truck?" I asked for a new one and he said it'll be here Saturday....4 days more without my couch. I left frustrated and ignored it. Spoke to them again on friday over the phone and asked if we can have the delivery drivers take it to my house without the $45 charge as compensation for delay and damaged goods. He refused and simply said, "it'll be here tomorrow, come pick it up tomorrow". Mixed Berry with dark mint chocolate - Best customization ever.  Such a simple idea and I'm shocked it hasn't caught on anywhere else.  I felt like the pop was more icy than sorbetish but it was tasty.

Friendly service and good with explanation on the process.

Ambiance: 4/5

It's a small shop but the outdoor seating is nice.< /review>

I had such an amazing experience surfing with Will. He is super calm, patient, clear & thorough in his instructions, helpful, and has tremendous physical strength & stamina, which was certainly needed on this crazy day! The current was stronger than I‚Äôve ever witnessed, and the waves were so monstrous, only very experienced surfers could be out in them, so we were restricted to the shallow ‚Äúfoamies,‚Äù which were so strong they were literally knocking me off me feet. I would have been carried away numerous times if Will hadn‚Äôt told me to get up on the board and he fought the current, dragging me & the board out to the waves. He did this repeatedly for 2 hours!! Dedication and stamina!
With his instruction, I was able to get up with every wave, even if I didn‚Äôt always stay up for very long. By the end of our 2 hour session, we were both pretty exhausted, and in my mind I knew it would be my last wave. Thankfully, it was the BEST wave and BEST ride I had all day! From start to finish, a great experience.  I was a little hesitant because there's no actual building to go to.  A van with all the boards and wetsuits and even sunscreen parks at the end of the street.  It worked out great.  Jason, who runs it and answers the phone, was professional and friendly and I felt confident by the end of the phone call that my kids were in good hands.  Because I booked for four, he threw in a second instructor for free so they'd all have more of a private lesson.  Next time, I'm including myself in the lesson!  The two instructors were top notch. <rate>5< /rate>< Review>
My daughter and I had a WONDERFUL experience with Learn to Surf. I called  the morning of, having decided to give myself a surf lesson for my birthday, and having a hard time finding anyone who could fit me in. Jason was determined to fit me in. Our instructor, Ben, could not have been nicer. I appreciated that he took technique and safety very seriously in the initial lesson on the sand. In the water he watched us closely and commented on what we could improve each time. When we were struggling with a certain part of getting up, he took us back to the sand to practice again. We were much improved after taking that break to fix our form. It was so fun and we learned so much! I actually loved that we just met them at a van--that I felt there was no unnecessary markup. The van had our wetsuits and boards, and we were able to lock our valuables in. I really liked the choice of beach, as it was a learning beach that wasn't intimidating. We will definitely be back for more lessons from Learn to Surf!<//Review>

< Text>
there were 4 of us that took lessons, first of all we had a GREAT TIME!!! there were 2 instructors, unfortunately I am very bad with names so I can't give their names but one instructor was from the Canary Islands the other was from San Clemente, anyone who is surfing for the first time probably knows that you do not learn to surf in 1 lesson, but I think what you are finding out is are you interested in continuing to learn, our instructors were incredibly nice and patient, as bad as we all were they continued to praise us any time we were even remotely  close to doing anything that resembled surfing, they even praised us for the effort we were giving, safety was their first order of business everything was explained in detail on shore and I felt confident that my family was safe while under the instruction of these two gentlemen, the boards were supplied as well as wet suits, we originally were scheduled to take the lesson at Huntington Beach, when we were called it was recommended that we take the lesson at Newport Beach because the current and waves were not as strong, that turned out to be a great suggestion as the location was much less crowded and the conditions were definitely  safer, I can't say enough good things about our experience, if you are planning lessons these are the right people, thanks for the great time and experience!</Text>

<UserId.>116523053311108791011<//UserId.><review>From Big Meadow trailhead to Scott's Lake is a great moderate hike for a person in moderately good shape. Some stepping up boulders but very good footing. Not too much altitude change on this leg of the TRT. You do have to walk/run across the freeway at the start. Pit toilets available at the trailhead with no posted trail map. The well trodden trail was easy to follow, but I didn't see blazes that you would need for snowshoeing.

Pretty Aspen trees.  The lake was low - my big dogs were still wading 15 feet from shore.  I ran into about 15 people on a Tuesday afternoon - four mountain bikers and the rest hikers.

Took me about 2 hours round trip at a brisk pace with a 15 minute break at the lake for the dogs to swim.</review><rate>5<//rate>< pics>

Came here for a Yelp event before the Fresno Foxes game and I will definitely be back. This place has delicious tasting craft beers. The great part is that it is actually family friendly. They have corn hole and a few games set up. Food trucks are available to grab a bite to eat. The food selection is definitely good. When I went they had gyros and a Cuban sandwiches. I got Cuban sandwiches and they were good. The awesome part was after the game, we were walking past to go to our car, and the security guards were welcoming us back in since we had our wrist bands. The atmosphere is enjoyable.  They have the DJ playing from the afternoon until closing. Definitely coming back</Review>

<name>Roberto Farias<//name><Date>1552853604558< /Date><Rate>5< /Rate><Review>Coolest spot in downtown Fresno without a doubt. It's incredible we have this brewery in the heart of the city. On any given night of the week there's an event. Either trivia night , loteria or live music. Most days they have a food truck. A few times if year they host special events and shut down the block. They have a game room now and they have corn hole and foosball. The beer is outstanding. The cure beers are solid and the new stuff they put out constantly is amazing. They have heaters and fire pit tables when it's cold and an awesome patio area when it's sunny. Swamp cooler when it inevitably gets to be super hot. Very dog friendly and often you'll see people bring their furry friends, myself included.This place is truly a gem in Fresno.<//Review>< pictures>

<userid>105018861016506182415<//userid>< Name>
L Kliew</Name>
<Time>1440600528276< /Time>< rate>
5<//rate>
< text>
We're from Northern California and discovering and enjoying local beer is one of our favorite activities. It is not often that we find ourselves in Fresno, but last weekend, there we were. Having been introduced to Tioga-Sequoia's "Half Dome" a wonderful, unfiltered California Wheat Ale, by a friend, we wanted to try their other offerings.  The brewery is downtown Fresno, and offers some of the finest brews I've tasted. Unlike most small brewers, Tioga Sequoia has a large number of beers to offer. Just to mention a few...Tamarack is a nice amber lager, 99 Golden Ale was my pick along with their Half Dome. Kathy couldn't get past the Cucumber Pilsner. Cucumber Pilsner? Yes, I tried it and like it too, it's crisp and lite and begs to be drank in the heat of the day.  Now if you think Cucumber is special...Try their Piece of Cake Stout!  You bet ya, Cake Stout, with it's hint of chocolate it's just what we needed for a upcoming birthday celebration. It was a Wow experience...we were very impressed with the fine folks and friendly reception that we were provided at Tioga-Sequoia Brewing. Oh Yea, the Beer is Great...we loaded up on the four beers I mentioned and headed back to Dixon...smiling all the way.< /text>
